Kaluza-Klein with varying scalar field


coordinate convention: $dx^0 = c dt, \partial_0 = \frac{1}{c} \partial_t$

$c = $ $\cdot \frac{m}{s} = 1 = $ the speed of light.
$G = $ $\cdot \frac{m^3}{kg \cdot s^2} = 1 = $ gravitational constant.
$k_e = $ $\cdot \frac{kg \cdot m^3}{C^2 \cdot s^2}$ = Coulomb's constant (typically $\frac{1}{4 \pi \epsilon_0}$).
$\sqrt{{\frac{1}{G}}{({{k_e}})}}$ = {=={ sqrt_Coulomb_constant_over_gravitational_constant_in_kg_per_C = Math.sqrt(Coulomb_constant_in_kg_m3_per_C2_s2 / gravitational_constant_in_m3_per_kg_s2) }==} $ \cdot \frac{kg}{C} = 1 =$ conversion from kg to C
$kg = $ {=={ 1 / sqrt_Coulomb_constant_over_gravitational_constant_in_kg_per_C }==} $C$.

${ A}_u$ = electromagnetic four-potential, in units $\frac{{{kg}} \cdot {{m}}}{{{C}} {{s}}}$
$A_5$ is constant in natural units, but to cancel the units of $\phi_K$ it is in units of $\frac{{{kg}} \cdot {{m}}}{{{C}} {{s}}}$ so $A_5$ is proportional to $c \sqrt{\frac{k_e}{G}} = $ ${{3.4789926447386\cdot{10^{18}}}} {{m}} {{kg}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{s}}} {{\frac{1}{C}}}$

${\phi_K}$ = scalar field, proportional to $\frac{1}{A_5}$, in units $\frac{{{C}} {{s}}}{{{kg}} \cdot {{m}}}$

${{ g}_{\mu}}_{\nu}$ = 4D metric tensor, with units $[g_{\mu\nu}] = 1$
${{ g}^{\mu}}^{\nu}$ = 4D metric inverse

${{ \tilde{g}}_a}_b$ = 5D metric tensor, with units $[\tilde{g}_{ab}] = 1$
${{{ \tilde{g}}_a}_b} = {\overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {{ \tilde{g}}_{\alpha}}_{\beta} & {{ \tilde{g}}_{\alpha}}_5 \\ {{ \tilde{g}}_5}_{\beta} & {{ \tilde{g}}_5}_5\end{matrix}\right]}}$
${{{ \tilde{g}}_a}_b} = {\overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {{{ g}_{\alpha}}_{\beta}} + {{{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} & {{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}}}} {{{ A}_5}} \\ {{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}}} {{{ A}_5}} & {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}}\end{matrix}\right]}}$


What is $u_5$ in terms of $u^5$?
${{ u}_5} = {{{{{ \tilde{g}}_5}_a}} {{{ u}^a}}}$
${{ u}_5} = {{{{{{ \tilde{g}}_5}_{\beta}}} {{{ u}^{\beta}}}} + {{{{{ \tilde{g}}_5}_5}} {{{ u}^5}}}}$
substitute definition of ${{ \tilde{g}}_a}_b$
${{ u}_5} = {{{{{{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}}} {{{ A}_5}}}} {{{ u}^{\beta}}}} + {{{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}}}} {{{ u}^5}}}}$


On a side note, later for the Lorentz force to arise we are going to set:
${{ u}^5} = {{{{{\frac{1}{4}}} {{{\frac{1}{M}}{({q})}}}}} {{\sqrt{{\frac{1}{G}}{({{k_e}})}}}}}$

For an electron this comes out to be...
$e =$ $\cdot C$ = electron charge
$m_e =$ $\cdot kg$ = electron mass
$u^5 = \frac{1}{4} \frac{q}{M} \sqrt{\frac{k_e}{G}} =$ {=={ u5U = .25 * electron_charge_in_C / electron_mass_in_kg * Math.sqrt(Coulomb_constant_in_kg_m3_per_C2_s2 / gravitational_constant_in_m3_per_kg_s2) }==} = {=={ u5U * speed_of_light_in_m_per_s }==} $\frac{m}{s}$.


What if we require a unit 5-velocity?
${{{{{ \tilde{g}}_a}_b}} {{{ u}^a}} {{{ u}^b}}} = {-{1}}$
split off spacetime indexes
${{{{{{{{{ \tilde{g}}_{\alpha}}_{\beta}}} {{{ u}^{\alpha}}}}} {{{ u}^{\beta}}}} + {{{{{{{2}} {{{{ \tilde{g}}_{\alpha}}_5}}}} {{{ u}^{\alpha}}}}} {{{ u}^5}}}} + {{{{{ \tilde{g}}_5}_5}} {{{{ u}^5}^{2}}}}} = {-1}$
Substitute definition of ${{ \tilde{g}}_a}_b$
${{{{{ u}^{\alpha}}} {{{{ g}_{\alpha}}_{\beta}}} {{{ u}^{\beta}}}} + {{{{ u}^{\alpha}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ u}^{\beta}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ u}^{\alpha}}} {{{ u}^5}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_5}}} + {{{{{ u}^5}^{2}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}}}} = {-{1}}$
Solve quadratic for ${{{ A}_5}} {{{ u}^5}}$ ...
${{ u}^5} = {{{\frac{1}{{ A}_5}}} {{({{ {-{{ A}_{\mu}}} {{{ u}^{\mu}}}} \pm {\sqrt{{{({{{{ A}_{\mu}}} {{{ u}^{\mu}}}})}^{2}} - {{{{{\phi_K}}^{-2}}} {{({{{{{ u}_{\mu}}} {{{ u}^{\mu}}}} + {1}})}}}}}})}}}$
Notice that if we assume $u_\mu u^\mu = -1$ then this simplifies to ${{ u}^5} = {{{{{{{-2}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{{ A}_5}}}}} {{{ A}_{\mu}}}}} {{{ u}^{\mu}}}}$ , however in reality things might instead be $u_\mu u^\mu \approx -1$

If we substitute our definition for $u^5$ then the solution of the quadratic looks like:
${{{{{\frac{1}{4}}} {{{\frac{1}{M}}{({q})}}}}} {{\sqrt{{\frac{1}{G}}{({{k_e}})}}}}} = {{{\frac{1}{{ A}_5}}} {{({{ {-{{ A}_{\mu}}} {{{ u}^{\mu}}}} \pm {\sqrt{{{({{{{ A}_{\mu}}} {{{ u}^{\mu}}}})}^{2}} - {{{{{\phi_K}}^{-2}}} {{({{{{{ u}_{\mu}}} {{{ u}^{\mu}}}} + {1}})}}}}}})}}}$
${{{q}} {{\frac{1}{M}}}} = {{{{-4}} {{{ A}_{\mu}}} {{{ u}^{\mu}}} {{{G}^{({\frac{1}{2}})}}} {{\frac{1}{{ A}_5}}} {{\frac{1}{{{k_e}}^{({\frac{1}{2}})}}}}} \pm {{{4}} {{ii}} \cdot {{{({{1} + {{{-1}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_{\mu}}^{2}}} {{{{ u}^{\mu}}^{2}}}} + {{{{ u}^{\mu}}} {{{ u}_{\mu}}}}})}^{({\frac{1}{2}})}}} {{{G}^{({\frac{1}{2}})}}} {{\frac{1}{{\phi_K}}}} {{\frac{1}{{ A}_5}}} {{\frac{1}{{{k_e}}^{({\frac{1}{2}})}}}}}}$
Let's look at the magnitude of this for some real-world values.
Electrons in a copper wire (from my 'magnetic field from a boosted charge' worksheet).
$N_A = $ $\cdot \frac{1}{mol}$ = Avogadro's constant.
$m_a =$ $\frac{g}{mol} =$ {=={atomic_mass_in_kg = 1e-3 * atomic_mass_in_g}==} $ \cdot \frac{kg}{mol} = $ atomic mass.
$n_v =$ nominal valency.
$\rho =$ $\frac{g}{cm^3} =$ {=={material_density_in_kg_per_m3 = material_density_in_g_per_cm3 * 1e+3}==} $\frac{kg}{m^3} = $ matter density.
$n_e = \frac{N_A \cdot n_v}{m_a} = $ {=={free_electrons_per_kg = Avogadro_constant_in_1_per_mol * material_nominal_valency / atomic_mass_in_kg}==} $\frac{e}{kg} = $ free electrons per kg.
$\rho_{charge} = n_e \cdot \rho = $ {=={electron_density_in_e_per_m3 = free_electrons_per_kg * material_density_in_kg_per_m3}==} $\frac{e}{m^3}$ = electron density.
$R =$ $mm =$ {=={wire_radius_in_m = wire_radius_in_mm * 1e-3}==} $m =$ wire radius.
$r = \sqrt{y^2 + z^2} =$ $m = $ distance of measurement from the wire along the x-axis.
$A = \pi R^2 =$ {=={wire_cross_section_area_in_m2 = Math.PI * wire_radius_in_m * wire_radius_in_m}==} $m^2 =$ wire cross-section area
$I =$ $A =$ current in wire.
$q = \rho_{charge} \cdot e =$ {=={charge_density_in_C_per_m3 = electron_density_in_e_per_m3 * electron_charge_in_C}==} $\frac{C}{m^3} = $ charge density.
$\lambda = A q = \pi R^2 \rho_{charge} e =$ {=={charge_per_unit_length_in_C_per_m = charge_density_in_C_per_m3 * wire_cross_section_area_in_m2}==} $\frac{C}{m}$ = charge density per unit meter along wire
$v = \frac{I}{\lambda} =$ {=={mean_electron_velocity_in_m_per_s = current_in_A / (wire_cross_section_area_in_m2 * charge_density_in_C_per_m3)}==} $\frac{C}{m} =$ charge density per unit meter along wire.
$\beta = \frac{v}{c} =$ {=={Lorentz_beta = mean_electron_velocity_in_m_per_s / speed_of_light_in_m_per_s}==} = unitless, spatial component of 4-velocity.
$\gamma = 1 / \sqrt{1 - \beta^2} \approx 1 + \frac{v^2}{2 c^2} \approx $ 1 + {=={Lorentz_gamma_minus_one = .5 * Lorentz_beta * Lorentz_beta}==} $\approx$ {=={Lorentz_gamma = 1 + Lorentz_gamma_minus_one}==} = Lorentz factor.
$E = 2 \lambda k_e \frac{1}{r} \frac{v^2}{c^2} = \frac{\lambda}{2 \pi \epsilon_0 r} \frac{v^2}{c^2} = 2 \pi R^2 \rho_{charge} e k_e \frac{1}{r} =$ {=={electric_field_in_kg_m2_per_C_s2 = charge_per_unit_length_in_C_per_m * 2 * Coulomb_constant_in_kg_m3_per_C2_s2 / field_measure_distance_in_m * (mean_electron_velocity_in_m_per_s * mean_electron_velocity_in_m_per_s) / (speed_of_light_in_m_per_s * speed_of_light_in_m_per_s)}==} $\cdot \frac{kg \cdot m}{C \cdot s^2}$ = electric field magnitude.
$B = \frac{1}{c} \beta \gamma E = $ {=={magnetic_field_in_kg_m_per_C_s = Lorentz_beta * Lorentz_gamma * (electric_field_in_kg_m2_per_C_s2 / speed_of_light_in_m_per_s) }==} $\frac{kg}{C \cdot s} =$ magnetic field magnitude.
$u^0 = \gamma, u^1 = \beta \gamma, u^2 = u^3 = 0$ = our 4-velocity components, such that $\eta_{\mu\nu} u^\mu u^\nu = -1$.
$\phi_q = \frac{1}{2} \lambda k_e ln ( \frac{r}{r_0} ) =$ electric potential.
... but what is $r_0$? The EM potential has a constant which does not influence 4D or 3D EM, but will influence 5D EM.

Let's look at the potential with and without the constant: $\phi_q = \phi'_q + \phi''_q$.
$\phi'_q = \frac{1}{2} \lambda k_e ln(r) =$ {=={ electric_potential_in_kg_m2_per_C_s2 = .5 * charge_density_in_C_per_m3 * Coulomb_constant_in_kg_m3_per_C2_s2 * Math.log(field_measure_distance_in_m) }==} $\frac{kg \cdot m^2}{C \cdot s^2}$.
$\phi''_q = \frac{1}{2} \lambda k_e ln(r_0) = $ arbitrary.
$A_i = 0 = $ magnetic vector potential.
So $A_\mu u^\mu = A_0 u^0 = \frac{1}{c} \phi_q \gamma = $ {=={ A_dot_u = electric_potential_in_kg_m2_per_C_s2 / speed_of_light_in_m_per_s * Lorentz_gamma }==} $ \frac{kg \cdot m}{C \cdot s} + \frac{1}{c} \phi''_q \gamma$.
And $\frac{1}{A_5} A_\mu u^\mu = $ {=={ A_dot_u_over_A5L = A_dot_u / A5L }==} $ + \frac{1}{c A_5} \phi''_q \gamma$

Assume $u_\mu u^\mu = -1$.
$u^5 = -2 \frac{1}{A_5} A_\mu u^\mu = $ {=={ -2 * A_dot_u_over_A5L }==} $ - \frac{1}{c A_5} \gamma \phi''_q$

Let's insert this into the $u^5$ equation above and solve to find what $\phi''_q$ would be:
$\frac{1}{c A_5} \gamma \phi''_q = \frac{1}{4} \frac{q}{M} \sqrt{\frac{k_e}{G}}$
$\phi''_q = \frac{1}{4} c^2 \frac{q}{\gamma m} \frac{k_e}{G} = \frac{1}{4} c^2 \frac{q}{M} \frac{k_e}{G} \sqrt{1 - \beta^2}$
Using our electron charge-to-mass ratio this gives us: $\phi''_q =$ {=={ u5U * speed_of_light_in_m_per_s * A5L / Lorentz_gamma }==} $\frac{kg \cdot m^2}{C \cdot s^2}$
...which is a few orders of magnitude higher than what contributes to the EM field.

So, assuming we want our 5-velocity to be normalized with the 5-metric, and assuming our 4-velocity is normalized with the 4-metric, then it looks like the 5th velocity is made up of two parts:
1) the EM potential, dot the negligible 4-vel, which is on the order of $10^{-12}$ for our current through a copper wire.
2) the the arbitrary constant, which must relate to the charge-mass ratio, which is on the order of $10^{21}$.
Also notice that this shows then the charge-mass ratio in the Lorentz force law will be influenced by the 3-velocity.

Of course you can avoid the constraint that that charge-mass ratio is dependent on the 3-velocity if you just relax the constraint of $u_\mu u^\mu = -1$.
Then, for constaint $u^5 = \frac{1}{4} \frac{q}{M} \sqrt{\frac{k_e}{G}}$, any deviations in the electric potential $A_t$ could relate to deviations in the 4-vel-norm (or in deviations in the Kaluza field, which I am keeping constant in this worksheet).

Let's look at $\delta u^5$ with respect to $\delta u^\mu$ in the constraint above:
$ \delta u^5 = -\frac{1}{(A_5)^2} \delta A_5 ( -A_\mu u^\mu \pm \sqrt{ (A_\mu u^\mu)^2 - {\phi_K}^{-2} ( u_\mu u^\mu + 1) } ) + \frac{1}{A_5} ( - \delta A_\mu u^\mu - A_\mu \delta u^\mu \pm \frac{ A_\mu u^\mu (\delta A_\mu u^\mu + A_\mu \delta u^\mu) + {\phi_K}^{-3} \delta \phi_K (u_\mu u^\mu + 1) - {\phi_K}^{-2} u_\mu \delta u^\mu }{\sqrt{ (A_\mu u^\mu)^2 - {\phi_K}^{-2} (u_\mu u^\mu + 1) }} ) $
...and as for $\delta u^5$ wrt $\delta (u_\mu u^\mu)$ in specific...
$ \frac{\delta u^5}{\delta (u_\mu u^\mu)} = \mp \frac{ 1 }{2 A_5 {\phi_K}^2 \sqrt{ (A_\mu u^\mu)^2 - {\phi_K}^{-2} (u_\mu u^\mu + 1) }} $
...and if $A_5 = 2 (\phi_K)^{-1}$...
$ \frac{\delta u^5}{\delta (u_\mu u^\mu)} = \mp \frac{ 1 }{4 \sqrt{ 4 (\frac{1}{A_5} A_\mu u^\mu)^2 - u_\mu u^\mu + 1 }} $



${{ \tilde{g}}^u}^v$ = 5D metric inverse
Notice, if you see a raised 4-index, it is being raised by the 4-metric and not the 5-metric.
${{{ \tilde{g}}^a}^b} = {\overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {{ g}^{\alpha}}^{\beta} & \frac{-{{ A}^{\alpha}}}{{ A}_5} \\ \frac{-{{ A}^{\beta}}}{{ A}_5} & {{({{{{{ A}_{\mu}}} {{{ A}^{\mu}}}} + {{{\phi_K}}^{-2}}})}} {{{{ A}_5}^{-2}}}\end{matrix}\right]}}$

${{{{{{ \tilde{g}}_a}_c}} {{{{ \tilde{g}}^c}^b}}} = {\overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}^{\beta}}}} - {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}^{\beta}}}}} + {{{ \delta}_{\alpha}}^{\beta}} & \frac{{{ A}_{\alpha}} + {{{{{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\delta}}} {{{ A}^{\delta}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}}} - {{ A}_{\alpha}}} - {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\delta}}} {{{ A}^{\delta}}}}}}{{ A}_5} \\ -{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{ A}^{\beta}} - {{ A}^{\beta}}})}}} & {{1} - {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\delta}}} {{{ A}^{\delta}}}}} + {{{{ A}_{\delta}}} {{{ A}^{\delta}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}}}\end{matrix}\right]}}} = {\overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {{ \delta}_{\alpha}}^{\beta} & 0 \\ 0 & 1\end{matrix}\right]}}$

The cylindrical constraint is
${{{{ \tilde{g}}_a}_b}_{,5}} = {0}$
Therefore
${\left[\begin{matrix} {{{{ g}_{\alpha}}_{\beta}}_{,5}} + {{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,5}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,5}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,5}}}} & {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,5}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_5}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,5}}}} + {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ A}_5}_{,5}}}}})}} \\ {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,5}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_5}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,5}}}} + {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{{ A}_5}_{,5}}}}})}} & {{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_5}_{,5}}}} + {{{{ A}_5}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,5}}}}})}}\end{matrix}\right]} = {0}$
Therefore, if $A_{5,5} = 0$ then we find:
${{ {\phi_K}}_{,5}} = {0}$
${{{ A}_{\mu}}_{,5}} = {0}$
${{{{ g}_{\alpha}}_{\beta}}_{,5}} = {0}$

metric partial:
${{{{ \tilde{g}}_a}_b}_{,c}} = {\overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {{{{ g}_{\alpha}}_{\beta}}_{,c}} + {{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,c}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,c}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,c}}}} & {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,c}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_5}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,c}}}} + {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ A}_5}_{,c}}}}})}} \\ {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,c}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_5}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,c}}}} + {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{{ A}_5}_{,c}}}}})}} & {{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_5}_{,c}}}} + {{{{ A}_5}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,c}}}}})}}\end{matrix}\right]}}$
${{{{ \tilde{g}}_a}_b}_{,c}} = {\overset{c\downarrow[{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}]}{\left[\begin{matrix} \overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {{{{ g}_{\alpha}}_{\beta}}_{,\gamma}} + {{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,\gamma}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,\gamma}}}} & {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}}}})}} \\ {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}}}})}} & {{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}}\end{matrix}\right]} \\ \overset{a\downarrow b\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} 0 & 0 \\ 0 & 0\end{matrix}\right]}\end{matrix}\right]}}$

lower connection
${{{{ \tilde{\Gamma}}_a}_b}_c} = {\overset{a\downarrow[{b\downarrow c\rightarrow}]}{\left[\begin{matrix} \overset{b\downarrow c\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {\frac{1}{2}}{({{{{{ g}_{\alpha}}_{\beta}}_{,\gamma}} + {{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,\gamma}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{{ g}_{\alpha}}_{\gamma}}_{,\beta}} + {{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\beta}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,\beta}}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}}} + {{{{{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ A}_{\gamma}}_{,\beta}}}} - {{{{ g}_{\beta}}_{\gamma}}_{,\alpha}}} - {{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}}}} - {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}}}} - {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{{ A}_{\gamma}}_{,\alpha}}}}}})} & {\frac{1}{2}}{({{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,\beta}}}} + {{{{{2}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\beta}}}} - {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,\alpha}}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\alpha}}}}}})}}})} \\ {\frac{1}{2}}{({{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\alpha}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{{{2}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}}} - {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\gamma}}_{,\alpha}}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\alpha}}}}}})}}})} & -{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\alpha}}}}\end{matrix}\right]} \\ \overset{b\downarrow c\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {\frac{1}{2}}{({{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\gamma}}_{,\beta}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\beta}}}}})}}})} & {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\beta}}} \\ {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}} & 0\end{matrix}\right]}\end{matrix}\right]}}$
${{{{ \tilde{\Gamma}}_a}_b}_c} = {\overset{a\downarrow[{b\downarrow c\rightarrow}]}{\left[\begin{matrix} \overset{b\downarrow c\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {\frac{1}{2}}{({{{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{{ F}_{\gamma}}_{\alpha}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\beta}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}} {{{{ F}_{\beta}}_{\alpha}}}} + {{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ A}_{\gamma}}_{,\beta}}}} - {{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}}}} + {{{2}} {{{{{ \Gamma}_{\alpha}}_{\beta}}_{\gamma}}}}})} & {\frac{1}{2}}{({{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{2}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\beta}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\alpha}}}}} + {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ F}_{\beta}}_{\alpha}}}}})}}})} \\ {\frac{1}{2}}{({{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{2}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}}} - {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\alpha}}}}} + {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ F}_{\gamma}}_{\alpha}}}}})}}})} & -{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\alpha}}}}\end{matrix}\right]} \\ \overset{b\downarrow c\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {\frac{1}{2}}{({{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ A}_5}} {{({{{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_{\gamma}}_{,\beta}}}} + {{{2}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\beta}}}}})}}})} & {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\beta}}} \\ {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}} & 0\end{matrix}\right]}\end{matrix}\right]}}$

upper connection
${{{{ \tilde{\Gamma}}^a}_b}_c} = {{{\overset{a\downarrow e\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {{ g}^{\alpha}}^{\epsilon} & \frac{-{{ A}^{\alpha}}}{{ A}_5} \\ \frac{-{{ A}^{\epsilon}}}{{ A}_5} & \frac{{1} + {{{{ A}_{\mu}}} {{{ A}^{\mu}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}}}}{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}}}\end{matrix}\right]}}} {{\overset{e\downarrow[{b\downarrow c\rightarrow}]}{\left[\begin{matrix} \overset{b\downarrow c\rightarrow}{\left[\begin{matrix} {\frac{1}{2}}{({{{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\gamma}}} {{{ A}_{\epsilon}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\beta}}} {{{{ F}_{\gamma}}_{\epsilon}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\epsilon}}} {{{{ A}_{\beta}}_{,\gamma}}}} + {{{2}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\beta}}} {{{ A}_{\epsilon}}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}}} + {{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\gamma}}} {{{{ F}_{\beta}}_{\epsilon}}}} + {{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\epsilon}}} {{{{ A}_{\gamma}}_{,\beta}}}} - stress-energy tensor:
$\tilde{G}_{ab} = \frac{8 \pi G}{c^4} T_{ab}$

\tilde{T}}_5}_{\beta}}} {{\frac{1}{{c}^{4}}}} & {{8}} {{\pi}} \cdot {{G}} {{{{ \tilde{T}}_5}_5}} {{\frac{1}{{c}^{4}}}}\end{matrix}\right]}}$


Looking at the $\tilde{G}_{55}$ components:
${{{{-3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{8}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{4}}} {{{{ F}_{\epsilon}}^{\zeta}}} {{{{ F}_{\zeta}}^{\epsilon}}}} + {{{-1}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{R}}}} = {{{8}} {{\pi}} \cdot {{G}} {{{{ \tilde{T}}_5}_5}} {{\frac{1}{{c}^{4}}}}}$
Isolating the $\tilde{T}_{55}$ stress-energy term:
${{{ \tilde{T}}_5}_5} = {{{{-3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{64}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{4}}} {{{c}^{4}}} {{{{ F}_{\epsilon}}^{\zeta}}} {{{{ F}_{\zeta}}^{\epsilon}}} {{\frac{1}{\pi}}} {{\frac{1}{G}}}} + {{{-1}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{16}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{c}^{4}}} {{R}} {{\frac{1}{\pi}}} {{\frac{1}{G}}}}}$
Isolating the spacetime scalar curvature R:
${R} = {{{{-16}} {{G}} {{\pi}} \cdot {{{{ \tilde{T}}_5}_5}} {{\frac{1}{{c}^{4}}}} {{\frac{1}{{{ A}_5}^{2}}}} {{\frac{1}{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}}}} + {{{-3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{4}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ F}_{\epsilon}}^{\zeta}}} {{{{ F}_{\zeta}}^{\epsilon}}}}}$
Look at it with our substituted values:
Substitute ${{ A}_5} = {{{c}} {{\sqrt{{\frac{1}{G}}{({{k_e}})}}}}}$, ${{k_e}} = {\frac{{{{\mu_0}}} \cdot {{{c}^{2}}}}{{{4}} {{\pi}}}}$
${R} = {{{{-64}} {{{G}^{2}}} {{{\pi}^{2}}} {{{{ \tilde{T}}_5}_5}} {{\frac{1}{{c}^{8}}}} {{\frac{1}{{\mu_0}}}} {{\frac{1}{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}}}} + {{{-3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{4}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ F}_{\epsilon}}^{\zeta}}} {{{{ F}_{\zeta}}^{\epsilon}}}}}$
It looks like $\tilde{T}_{55}$ provides the scalar curvature information ... with the exception of that extra term
What is the magnitude of that extra term?


Looking at the $\tilde{G}_{5\mu}$ components:
${{{{3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{ A}_5}} {{{\phi_K}}} \cdot {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\epsilon}}} {{{{ F}_{\alpha}}^{\epsilon}}}} + {{{-1}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{ A}_5}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{R}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}}} + {{{-3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{8}}} {{{ A}_5}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{4}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ F}_{\epsilon}}^{\zeta}}} {{{{ F}_{\zeta}}^{\epsilon}}}} + {{{\frac{1}{2}}} {{{ A}_5}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{{ F}_{\alpha}}^{\epsilon}}_{;\epsilon}}}}} = {{{8}} {{\pi}} \cdot {{G}} {{{{ \tilde{T}}_{\alpha}}_5}} {{\frac{1}{{c}^{4}}}}}$
Isolating the Faraday tensor divergence:
${{{{ F}_{\alpha}}^{\epsilon}}_{;\epsilon}} = {{{{R}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}}} + {{{16}} {{\pi}} \cdot {{G}} {{{{ \tilde{T}}_{\alpha}}_5}} {{\frac{1}{{c}^{4}}}} {{\frac{1}{{ A}_5}}} {{\frac{1}{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}}}} + {{{-3}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\epsilon}}} {{{{ F}_{\alpha}}^{\epsilon}}} {{\frac{1}{{\phi_K}}}}} + {{{3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{4}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ F}_{\epsilon}}^{\zeta}}} {{{{ F}_{\zeta}}^{\epsilon}}}}}$

And that conveniently cancelled a term. Now let's substitute the definition of $\tilde{T}_{55}$

Now to take a detour and write the stress-energy in terms of the four-current to see the Gauss-Ampere laws emerge:
Bring back the scalar curvature term R from $\tilde{T}_{55}$ and rewrite $\tilde{T}_{5\alpha}$ in terms of five-momentum:
Substitute ${{{ \tilde{T}}_5}_5} = {{{{-3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{64}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{4}}} {{{c}^{4}}} {{{{ F}_{\epsilon}}^{\zeta}}} {{{{ F}_{\zeta}}^{\epsilon}}} {{\frac{1}{\pi}}} {{\frac{1}{G}}}} + {{{-1}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{16}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{c}^{4}}} {{R}} {{\frac{1}{\pi}}} {{\frac{1}{G}}}}}$, ${{{ \tilde{T}}_{\alpha}}_5} = {{{{{{{{c}^{2}}} {{\rho}}}} {{{ u}_5}}}} {{{ u}_{\alpha}}}}$, ${{ u}_5} = {{{{{{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\epsilon}}}}} {{{ A}_5}}}} {{{ u}^{\epsilon}}}} + {{{{{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{{ A}_5}^{2}}}}} {{{ u}^5}}}}$, ${{ u}^5} = {{{{{\frac{1}{4}}} {{{\frac{1}{M}}{({q})}}}}} {{\sqrt{{\frac{1}{G}}{({{k_e}})}}}}}$, ${{ A}_5} = {{{c}} {{\sqrt{{\frac{1}{G}}{({{k_e}})}}}}}$, ${{k_e}} = {\frac{{{{\mu_0}}} \cdot {{{c}^{2}}}}{{{4}} {{\pi}}}}$
${{{{ F}_{\alpha}}^{\epsilon}}_{;\epsilon}} = {{{{3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{4}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ F}_{\epsilon}}^{\zeta}}} {{{{ F}_{\zeta}}^{\epsilon}}}} + {{{R}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}}} + {{{-3}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\epsilon}}} {{{{ F}_{\alpha}}^{\epsilon}}} {{\frac{1}{{\phi_K}}}}} + {{{16}} {{G}} {{\pi}} \cdot {{\rho}} \cdot {{{ u}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\epsilon}}} {{{ u}^{\epsilon}}} {{\frac{1}{{c}^{2}}}}} + {{{q}} {{\rho}} \cdot {{{\mu_0}}} \cdot {{c}} {{{ u}_{\alpha}}} {{\frac{1}{M}}}}}$
Define our four-current as ${{ J}_{\alpha}} = {{{{{{{c}} {{{\frac{1}{M}}{({q})}}}}} {{\rho}}}} {{{ u}_{\alpha}}}}$
${{{{ F}_{\alpha}}^{\epsilon}}_{;\epsilon}} = {{{{16}} {{G}} {{\pi}} \cdot {{\rho}} \cdot {{{ u}_{\alpha}}} {{{ A}_{\epsilon}}} {{{ u}^{\epsilon}}} {{\frac{1}{{c}^{2}}}}} + {{{R}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}}} + {{{{\mu_0}}} \cdot {{{ J}_{\alpha}}}} + {{{-3}} {{{ {\phi_K}}_{,\epsilon}}} {{{{ F}_{\alpha}}^{\epsilon}}} {{\frac{1}{{\phi_K}}}}} + {{{3}} \cdot {{\frac{1}{4}}} {{{{\phi_K}}^{2}}} {{{ A}_{\alpha}}} {{{{ F}_{\epsilon}}^{\zeta}}} {{{{ F}_{\zeta}}^{\epsilon}}}}}$
Move all but current to the left side:
